***dij.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dij.html>dij</a> (16138)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thio</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þeuhą</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language"><a href = vnd.unilang:west.html>West</a> Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">tsjea</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:thigh.html>thigh</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">þjó</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:close.html>close</a></span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:dei.html>Dei</a> stod <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dikt.html>dikt</a></b> attmed kvarandre.</i>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:they.html>They</a> stood <a href = vnd.unilang:close.html>close</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:each.html>each</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:other.html>other</a>.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">dîner</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <small>[<a href = vnd.unilang:term.html>Term</a>?]</small>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">disner</i>.

***dino.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dino.html>dino</a> (14156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:likely.html>Likely</a> borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dino.html>dino</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> clipping <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dinosaurus.html>dinosaurus</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:term.html>term</a> became <a href = vnd.unilang:especially.html>especially</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:prominent.html>prominent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:after.html>after</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:release.html>release</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jurassic_Park" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Jurassic Park">Jurassic <a href = vnd.unilang:park.html>Park</a></a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> 1993, <a href = vnd.unilang:but.html>but</a> predated <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:least.html>least</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:one.html>one</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:two.html>two</a> years.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dino.html>dino</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dino.html>dino</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:s.html>s</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dino.html>dinootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dino.html>dino</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dinosaur.html>dinosaur</a>; archosaur <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> super-order Dinosauria. <span class="defdate">[<a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:late.html>late</a> 20th <a href = vnd.unilang:c.html>c</a>.]</span></li></ol>
